    const { modals, toggleModal, operations, selectedItems, setSelectedItems, showToast, openConfirm } = useApp();
    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ type: 'inquiry', sender: '', subject: '', content: '', receivedDate: formatDateLocal(new Date()) });
    const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
    useEffect(() => { if (modals.inquiry) { if (selectedItems.inquiry) { setFormData({ type: selectedItems.inquiry.type || 'inquiry', sender: selectedItems.inquiry.sender || '', subject: selectedItems.inquiry.subject || '', content: selectedItems.inquiry.content || '', receivedDate: selectedItems.inquiry.receivedDate || formatDateLocal(new Date()) }); } else { setFormData({ type: 'inquiry', sender: '', subject: '', content: '', receivedDate: formatDateLocal(new Date()) }); } } }, [modals.inquiry, selectedItems.inquiry]);
    if (!modals.inquiry) return null;
    const handleSubmit = async () => { if (!formData.sender) { showToast('발신자를 입력해주세요.', 'error'); return; } setIsSaving(true); const saveData = { ...formData, id: selectedItems.inquiry?.id, category: 'inquiry' }; if (await operations.saveManagement(saveData, 'inquiry')) { showToast('저장되었습니다.'); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, inquiry: null})); toggleModal('inquiry', false); } else { showToast('저장 실패', 'error'); } setIsSaving(false); };
    const handleDelete = () => { if (!selectedItems.inquiry?.id) return; openConfirm('삭제하시겠습니까?', async () => { if (await operations.deleteManagement(selectedItems.inquiry.id)) { showToast('삭제되었습니다.'); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, inquiry: null})); toggleModal('inquiry', false); } }); };
    return (<div className="fixed inset-0 z-[100] flex items-center justify-center bg-[#42392e]/50 backdrop-blur-sm p-4"><div className="vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-xl border border-[#d4c4ac] overflow-hidden"><div className="p-5 flex justify-between items-center border-b border-[#d4c4ac] bg-[#f0e9de]"><div className="flex items-center gap-3"><div className="p-2 rounded-xl bg-[#a0714a] text-[#faf6ef]"><Mail size={20}/></div><div><h3 className="font-bold text-lg text-[#42392e]">{selectedItems.inquiry ? '메일 수정' : '메일 등록'}</h3><p className="text-xs text-[#857460]">외부 메일을 아카이브합니다</p></div></div><button onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, inquiry: null})); toggleModal('inquiry', false); }} className="p-2 hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] rounded-full"><X size={20} className="text-[#857460]"/></button></div><div className="p-5 space-y-4"><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] mb-2">분류</label><div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">{Object.entries(INQUIRY_CATEGORIES).map(([key, val]) => (<button key={key} type="button" onClick={() => setFormData({...formData, type: key})} className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold border ${formData.type === key ? val.color : 'bg-[#f0e9de] text-[#857460] border-[#d4c4ac]'}`}>{val.label}</button>))}</div></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] mb-2">발신자</label><input placeholder="예: ○○기업" value={formData.sender} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, sender: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl text-sm text-[#42392e] placeholder-[#78716c] focus:outline-none focus:border-[#a0714a]"/></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] mb-2">수신일</label><input type="date" value={formData.receivedDate} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, receivedDate: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl text-sm text-[#42392e] focus:outline-none focus:border-[#a0714a]"/></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] mb-2">제목</label><input placeholder="메일 제목" value={formData.subject} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, subject: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl text-sm text-[#42392e] placeholder-[#78716c] focus:outline-none focus:border-[#a0714a]"/></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] mb-2">내용</label><textarea placeholder="메일 내용을 복붙하세요..." value={formData.content} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, content: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl text-sm text-[#42392e] placeholder-[#78716c] h-40 resize-none focus:outline-none focus:border-[#a0714a]"/></div></div><div className="p-4 border-t border-[#d4c4ac] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#f0e9de]">{selectedItems.inquiry ? (<button onClick={handleDelete} className="px-4 py-2 text-[#9b4d4d] hover:bg-[#9b4d4d]/20 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center gap-1"><Trash size={14}/>삭제</button>) : <div/>}<div className="flex gap-2"><button onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, inquiry: null})); toggleModal('inquiry', false); }} className="px-4 py-2 text-[#857460] hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] rounded-lg text-sm font-bold">취소</button><button onClick={handleSubmit} disabled={isSaving} className="px-6 py-2 vj-btn-primary text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-lg text-sm flex items-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">{isSaving ? <Loader size={14} className="animate-spin"/> : <Save size={14}/>}저장</button></div></div></div></div>);
};

const PlanModal = () => {
    const { modals, toggleModal, selectedItems, setSelectedItems, profile, tasks, operations, showToast, openConfirm } = useApp();
    const { plan: initialData } = selectedItems;
    const [tab, setTab] = useState('basic');
    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ topic: '', type: 'main', uploadDate: '', description: '', planner: profile || '', status: 'draft', script: '', shootType: 'indoor', location: '' });
    const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
    const [isFullScreen, setIsFullScreen] = useState(false);
    const [isScriptMode, setIsScriptMode] = useState(false);
    const [pendingTasks, setPendingTasks] = useState([]);
    const [newTask, setNewTask] = useState({ author: '', category: [], start: formatDateLocal(new Date()), end: formatDateLocal(new Date()), detail: '' });

    useEffect(() => { 
        if(modals.plan) {
            if (initialData) {
                setFormData({ ...initialData, status: initialData.status || 'draft', script: initialData.script || '', shootType: initialData.shootType || 'indoor', location: initialData.location || '' });
            } else {
                setFormData({ topic: '', type: 'main', uploadDate: '', description: '', planner: profile || DEFAULT_AUTHOR, status: 'draft', script: '', shootType: 'indoor', location: '' });
            }
            setTab('basic'); setPendingTasks([]); setNewTask({ author: profile || DEFAULT_AUTHOR, category: [], start: formatDateLocal(new Date()), end: formatDateLocal(new Date()), detail: '' });
        } 
    }, [modals.plan, profile, initialData]);

    const handleAddPendingTask = () => {
        const currentAuthor = newTask.author?.trim(); const currentDetail = newTask.detail?.trim();
        if (!currentAuthor || !currentDetail) { showToast("담당자와 내용을 입력해주세요.", 'error'); return; }
        const taskToAdd = { ...newTask, author: currentAuthor, detail: currentDetail, id: Date.now() };
        setPendingTasks(prev => [...prev, taskToAdd]); setNewTask(prev => ({ ...prev, detail: '' }));
    };
    const handleRemovePendingTask = (id) => { setPendingTasks(pendingTasks.filter(t => t.id !== id)); };
    if (!modals.plan) return null;

    const handleSubmit = async (e, forceStatus) => { 
        e.preventDefault(); 
        if (forceStatus && !initialData?.id) { showToast("오류: 저장되지 않은 기획안은 상태를 변경할 수 없습니다. 먼저 저장해주세요.", 'error'); return; }
        setIsSaving(true); 
        const nextStatus = forceStatus || formData.status;
        const finalData = { ...formData, location: formData.shootType === 'indoor' ? '' : formData.location, status: nextStatus, id: initialData?.id };
        const res = await operations.savePlan(finalData);
        if(res.success) {
            const planId = res.id;
            if (pendingTasks.length > 0) {
                 for (const t of pendingTasks) {
                     // [FIX] 신규 생성 시 참조 검증 스킵 (skipPlanCheck: true)
                     await operations.saveTask({
                         planId: planId,
                         topic: formData.topic,
                         details: t.detail,
                         status: nextStatus === 'active' ? 'in_progress' : 'todo',
                         workStartDate: t.start,
                         workEndDate: t.end,
                         author: t.author,
                         type: 'task',
                         category: t.category,
                         isDraftPlaceholder: false,
                         skipPlanCheck: true 
                     }, false, false, false);
                 }
            }
            setIsSaving(false); toggleModal('plan', false);
            if ((forceStatus === 'active' || nextStatus === 'active') && (!initialData || initialData.status === 'draft')) { showToast("기획이 승인되었습니다. 제작이 시작됩니다!"); } else if (forceStatus === 'completed') { showToast("프로젝트가 완료 처리되었습니다."); } else { showToast("저장되었습니다."); }
        } else { setIsSaving(false); showToast("오류 발생", 'error'); }
    };

    const handleDelete = async () => { if (!initialData) return; openConfirm("이 기획안과 연결된 모든 일정을 영구 삭제하시겠습니까?\n이 작업은 되돌릴 수 없습니다.", async () => { const result = await operations.deletePlan(initialData.id, initialData.topic); if (result) { showToast("기획안이 삭제되었습니다."); toggleModal('plan', false); } else { showToast("삭제 실패", 'error'); } }); };
    const relatedTasks = initialData ? tasks.filter(t => t.planId === initialData.id).sort((a,b) => new Date(a.workStartDate) - new Date(b.workStartDate)) : [];
    const statusBadge = formData.status === 'draft' ? <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#e8dcc8] text-[#5a4d40] px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-bold">기획(Draft)</span> : (formData.status === 'completed' ? <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#5d7a5d]/20 text-[#4d6a4d] px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-bold">완료(Done)</span> : <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#5d6a7a]/20 text-[#4d5a6a] px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-bold">진행중(Active)</span>);

    const FullScreenEditor = () => (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-[200] bg-[#faf6ef] flex flex-col animate-in fade-in zoom-in-95 duration-200">
            <div className="p-4 border-b border-[#e8dcc8] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#faf6ef]"><h3 className="font-bold text-lg text-[#42392e] flex items-center gap-2"><FileText size={20}/> 기획안 전체화면</h3><button onClick={() => setIsScriptMode(false)} className="p-2 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-[#6a5d50] hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] font-bold text-sm flex items-center gap-2"><Minimize2 size={16}/> 닫기</button></div><div className="flex-1 p-6 bg-[#faf6ef] overflow-hidden flex flex-col"><RichTextEditor className="flex-1 shadow-sm h-full" value={formData.script} onChange={(val) => setFormData(prev => ({...prev, script: val}))} placeholder="여기에 기획 내용, 대본, 큐시트를 작성하세요." /></div>
        </div>
    );

    return (
        <div className={`fixed inset-0 z-[100] flex items-center justify-center bg-[#3a2d20]/30 backdrop-blur-sm p-4 ${isFullScreen ? 'p-0' : 'p-4'}`}>
            {isScriptMode && <FullScreenEditor />}
            <div className={`bg-[#faf6ef] w-full rounded-2xl shadow-2xl flex flex-col transition-all duration-300 ${isFullScreen ? 'h-full w-full max-w-none rounded-none' : 'max-w-3xl max-h-[90vh]'}`}>
                <div className="p-5 border-b border-[#e8dcc8] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-t-2xl"><div className="flex items-center gap-3"><div className="bg-[#4d5a6a] text-[#faf6ef] p-2 rounded-lg"><Layout size={20}/></div><div><h3 className="font-bold text-lg text-[#42392e]">{initialData ? '프로젝트 기획 수정' : '새 프로젝트 기획'}</h3><div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-0.5">{statusBadge} <span className="text-xs text-[#857460]">작성자: {formData.planner}</span></div></div></div><div className="flex gap-2">{initialData && (<button onClick={handleDelete} className="p-2 text-[#9b4d4d] hover:bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 rounded-full"><Trash size={20}/></button>)}<button onClick={() => setIsFullScreen(!isFullScreen)} className="p-2 text-[#857460] hover:text-[#4d5a6a] hover:bg-[#5d6a7a]/10 rounded-full transition-colors">{isFullScreen ? <Minimize2 size={20}/> : <Maximize2 size={20}/>}</button><button onClick={() => toggleModal('plan', false)} className="p-2 text-[#857460] hover:text-[#8b3d3d] hover:bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 rounded-full transition-colors"><X size={20}/></button></div></div>
                <div className="flex border-b border-[#e8dcc8] px-6 pt-4 gap-6 bg-[#faf6ef] sticky top-0 z-10"><button onClick={() => setTab('basic')} className={`pb-3 text-sm font-bold border-b-2 transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 ${tab === 'basic' ? 'border-[#4d5a6a] text-[#4d5a6a]' : 'border-transparent text-[#857460] hover:text-[#5a4d40]'}`}><StickyNote size={16}/> 기본 정보</button><button onClick={() => setTab('detail')} className={`pb-3 text-sm font-bold border-b-2 transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 ${tab === 'detail' ? 'border-[#4d5a6a] text-[#4d5a6a]' : 'border-transparent text-[#857460] hover:text-[#5a4d40]'}`}><FileText size={16}/> 상세 기획 / 대본</button><button onClick={() => setTab('schedule')} className={`pb-3 text-sm font-bold border-b-2 transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 ${tab === 'schedule' ? 'border-[#4d5a6a] text-[#4d5a6a]' : 'border-transparent text-[#857460] hover:text-[#5a4d40]'}`}><Briefcase size={16}/> 일정 관리 ({relatedTasks.length + pendingTasks.length})</button></div>
                <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 bg-[#faf6ef]">
                    {tab === 'basic' && (<div className="flex flex-col gap-6"><div className="bg-[#faf6ef] p-6 rounded-xl border border-[#d4c4ac] shadow-sm space-y-5"><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">프로젝트 구분</label><div className="flex gap-3">{Object.entries(PROJECT_TYPES).map(([key, config]) => {const Icon = config.icon; const isSelected = formData.type === key; return (<button key={key} type="button" onClick={() => setFormData({...formData, type: key})} className={`flex-1 py-4 rounded-xl border-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 font-bold transition-all ${isSelected ? config.color + ' border-current ring-2 ring-offset-1 ring-current shadow-md' : 'border-[#e8dcc8] bg-[#faf6ef] text-[#857460] hover:bg-[#f5f0e6]'}`}><Icon size={18}/> {config.label}</button>)})}</div></div><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">프로젝트 주제 (제목)</label><input required value={formData.topic || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, topic: e.target.value})} placeholder="예: 25SS 시즌 룩북 영상 제작" className="w-full p-4 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] font-bold text-lg text-[#32291e]"/></div><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">촬영 유형</label><div className="flex gap-3 mb-3"><button type="button" onClick={() => setFormData({...formData, shootType: 'indoor'})} className={`flex-1 py-3 px-4 rounded-xl border flex items-center justify-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold transition-all ${formData.shootType === 'indoor' ? 'bg-[#4a3d30] text-[#faf6ef] border-slate-800 shadow-md' : 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#d4c4ac] text-[#6a5d50] hover:bg-[#faf6ef]'}`}><Briefcase size={16} /> 내부 스튜디오</button><button type="button" onClick={() => setFormData({...formData, shootType: 'outdoor'})} className={`flex-1 py-3 px-4 rounded-xl border flex items-center justify-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold transition-all ${formData.shootType === 'outdoor' ? 'bg-[#5d7a5d] text-[#faf6ef] border-[#5d7a5d] shadow-md' : 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#d4c4ac] text-[#6a5d50] hover:bg-[#faf6ef]'}`}><MapPin size={16} /> 외부 로케이션</button></div>{formData.shootType === 'outdoor' && (<div><textarea value={formData.location || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, location: e.target.value})} placeholder={`촬영 장소 및 세부 정보를 입력하세요.`} className="w-full p-4 bg-[#5d7a5d]/10 border border-[#5d7a5d]/40 rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d7a5d] font-medium text-sm text-[#5d7a5d] placeholder-[#5d7a5d]/60 h-32 resize-none leading-relaxed"/></div>)}</div><div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4"><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">업로드 예정일</label><input required type="date" value={formData.uploadDate || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, uploadDate: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] font-mono text-sm text-[#32291e]"/></div><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">기획 담당자</label><input type="text" value={formData.planner || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, planner: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] font-bold text-[#32291e]"/></div></div><div><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase">기획 의도 (간략)</label><textarea value={formData.description || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, description: e.target.value})} placeholder="기획 의도를 간략히 입력하세요." className="w-full p-4 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] h-24 resize-none leading-relaxed text-sm text-[#32291e]"/></div></div></div>)}
                    {tab === 'detail' && (<div className="flex flex-col gap-6 h-full"><div className="bg-[#faf6ef] p-6 rounded-xl border border-[#d4c4ac] shadow-sm flex flex-col flex-1 min-h-[400px]"><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-2 block uppercase flex justify-between items-center"><span>🎥 상세 기획 내용 (대본/큐시트)</span><button onClick={() => setIsScriptMode(true)} className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] bg-[#5d6a7a]/10 text-[#4d5a6a] px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-bold hover:bg-[#5d6a7a]/20 transition-colors"><Maximize2 size={10}/> 크게 보기</button></label><RichTextEditor className="flex-1 min-h-[300px]" value={formData.script} onChange={(val) => setFormData(prev => ({...prev, script: val}))} placeholder="여기에 기획 내용, 대본, 큐시트를 작성하세요." /></div></div>)}
                    {tab === 'schedule' && (<div className="bg-[#faf6ef] p-6 rounded-xl border border-[#d4c4ac] shadow-sm"><div className="mb-6 p-4 bg-[#5d6a7a]/10/50 rounded-xl border border-[#5d6a7a]/30"><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#4d5a6a] uppercase flex items-center gap-1 mb-3"><Plus size={12}/> 세부 일정 추가</label><div className="space-y-3"><div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2"><input placeholder="담당자" value={newTask.author} onChange={e => setNewTask({...newTask, author: e.target.value})} className="p-2 border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]" /><input placeholder="업무 내용" value={newTask.detail} onChange={e => setNewTask({...newTask, detail: e.target.value})} className="p-2 border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]" /></div><div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2"><input type="date" value={newTask.start} onChange={e => setNewTask({...newTask, start: e.target.value})} className="p-2 border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]" /><input type="date" value={newTask.end} onChange={e => setNewTask({...newTask, end: e.target.value})} className="p-2 border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]" /></div><button type="button" onClick={handleAddPendingTask} className="w-full py-2 bg-[#4d5a6a] text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-[#3d4a5a]">리스트에 추가</button></div></div><div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] uppercase flex items-center gap-1">업무 일정 목록 ({relatedTasks.length + pendingTasks.length})</label></div><div className="space-y-2 max-h-[300px] overflow-y-auto">{pendingTasks.map(task => (<div key={task.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-[#5d6a7a]/10 rounded-xl border border-[#5d6a7a]/40"><div className="flex flex-col"><span className="text-xs font-bold text-blue-800">{task.detail} <span className="text-[#5d6a7a] font-normal">({task.author})</span></span><span className="text-[10px] text-[#5d6a7a]">{task.start} ~ {task.end}</span></div><button type="button" onClick={() => handleRemovePendingTask(task.id)} className="text-[#857460] hover:text-[#9b4d4d]"><X size={16}/></button></div>))}{relatedTasks.length > 0 ? relatedTasks.map(task => (<div key={task.id} onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-xl border border-[#e8dcc8] hover:border-[#5d6a7a]/50 cursor-pointer group transition-all"><div className="flex items-center gap-3"><div className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${task.status === 'done' ? 'bg-[#5d7a5d]' : task.status === 'in_progress' ? 'bg-[#5d6a7a]' : 'bg-[#d4c4ac]'}`}></div><div className="flex flex-col"><span className="text-xs font-bold text-[#4a3d30]">{task.details}</span><span className="text-[10px] text-[#857460]">{task.workStartDate} ~ {task.workEndDate} • {task.author}</span></div></div><ArrowRight size={14} className="text-slate-300 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"/></div>)) : (pendingTasks.length === 0 && <div className="text-center py-10 text-xs text-[#857460] bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-xl border border-dashed border-[#d4c4ac]">등록된 업무 일정이 없습니다.</div>)}</div></div>)}
                </div>
                <div className="p-5 border-t border-[#e8dcc8] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-b-2xl"><div className="text-xs text-[#857460] font-medium">{formData.status === 'draft' ? '📢 현재 기획 단계입니다.' : (formData.status === 'completed' ? '🎉 완료된 프로젝트입니다.' : '✅ 제작이 승인된 프로젝트입니다.')}</div><div className="flex gap-3">{formData.status === 'draft' && initialData && (<button onClick={(e) => handleSubmit(e, 'active')} className="px-5 py-2.5 bg-[#5a4d6a] text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-xl shadow-lg hover:bg-[#4a3d5a] hover:scale-105 transition-all flex items-center gap-2 "><Star size={16}/> 기획 승인 / 제작 착수</button>)}{formData.status === 'active' && initialData && (<button onClick={(e) => handleSubmit(e, 'completed')} className="px-5 py-2.5 bg-emerald-600 text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-xl shadow-lg hover:bg-emerald-700 hover:scale-105 transition-all flex items-center gap-2"><Archive size={16}/> 프로젝트 완료 처리</button>)}<button onClick={() => toggleModal('plan', false)} className="px-5 py-2.5 text-[#6a5d50] font-bold hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] rounded-xl transition-colors">닫기</button><button onClick={handleSubmit} disabled={isSaving} className="px-6 py-2.5 bg-[#3a2d20] text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-xl shadow-md hover:bg-[#5a4d40] transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">{isSaving ? <Loader size={18} className="animate-spin"/> : <Save size={18}/>} {initialData ? '저장' : '기획안 생성'}</button></div></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

const ScheduleModal = () => {
    const { modals, toggleModal, selectedItems, setSelectedItems, profile, operations, showToast, plans, selectedDate, filteredTasks, openConfirm } = useApp();
    const [mode, setMode] = useState('list'); const [tab, setTab] = useState('work'); 
    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ author: DEFAULT_AUTHOR, category: [], details: '', workStartDate: '', workEndDate: '', status: 'todo', planId: '', type: 'task', completedDates: [] });
    const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false); const [syncGroup, setSyncGroup] = useState(true);
    const dateRange = useMemo(() => { if (formData.workStartDate && formData.workEndDate) return getDatesInRange(formData.workStartDate, formData.workEndDate); return []; }, [formData.workStartDate, formData.workEndDate]);
    
    // [최적화] dailyTasks 필터링
    const dailyTasks = useMemo(() => { 
        if (!selectedDate || !filteredTasks) return []; 
        return filteredTasks.filter(t => !t.isDraftPlaceholder && t.workStartDate <= selectedDate && t.workEndDate >= selectedDate)
            .sort((a, b) => { if (a.status === 'done' && b.status !== 'done') return 1; if (a.status !== 'done' && b.status === 'done') return -1; return 0; }); 
    }, [selectedDate, filteredTasks]);

    useEffect(() => {
        if (modals.schedule) {
            if (selectedItems.task) {
                const initTask = selectedItems.task;
                setFormData({ ...initTask, workStartDate: initTask.workStartDate || selectedDate || formatDateLocal(new Date()), workEndDate: initTask.workEndDate || selectedDate || formatDateLocal(new Date()), category: initTask.category || [], planId: initTask.planId || '', type: initTask.type || 'task', author: initTask.author || profile || DEFAULT_AUTHOR, status: initTask.status || 'in_progress', completedDates: initTask.completedDates || [] });
                setMode(initTask.id ? 'edit' : 'create'); setTab(initTask.type === 'personal' ? 'personal' : 'work'); setSyncGroup(!!initTask.groupId);
            } else { setMode('list'); const defaultDate = selectedDate || formatDateLocal(new Date()); setFormData({ author: profile || DEFAULT_AUTHOR, category: [], details: '', workStartDate: defaultDate, workEndDate: defaultDate, status: 'in_progress', planId: '', type: 'task', completedDates: [] }); setSyncGroup(false); }
        }
    }, [modals.schedule, selectedItems.task, profile, selectedDate]);
    if (!modals.schedule) return null;

    const handleCreate = (type) => { setTab(type === 'personal' ? 'personal' : 'work'); const defaultDate = selectedDate || formatDateLocal(new Date()); setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, author: profile || DEFAULT_AUTHOR, category: type === 'personal' ? ['연차'] : ['대본'], details: '', status: type === 'personal' ? 'done' : 'in_progress', planId: type === 'task' && plans.length > 0 ? plans[0].id : '', type: type, workStartDate: defaultDate, workEndDate: defaultDate, completedDates: [] })); setMode('create'); };
    const handleSaveInternal = async () => { 
        setIsSaving(true); 
        const result = await operations.saveTask({ ...formData, id: selectedItems.task?.id }, mode === 'edit', false, syncGroup); 
        setIsSaving(false); 
        if (result.success) { 
            showToast(result.message); 
            if (selectedItems.task && selectedItems.task.id) toggleModal('schedule', false); else setMode('list'); 
        } else { 
            showToast(result.message || "저장 실패", 'error'); 
        } 
    };
    const toggleDateCompletion = async (dateStr) => { if (!formData.id) return; let newCompletedDates = [...(formData.completedDates || [])]; if (newCompletedDates.includes(dateStr)) { newCompletedDates = newCompletedDates.filter(d => d !== dateStr); } else { newCompletedDates.push(dateStr); } setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, completedDates: newCompletedDates })); await operations.saveTask({ ...formData, completedDates: newCompletedDates, id: selectedItems.task?.id }, true, false, !!formData.groupId); };
    const toggleCategory = (cat, isPersonal = false) => { setFormData(prev => { if (isPersonal) return { ...prev, category: [cat] }; const current = prev.category || []; if (current.includes(cat)) return { ...prev, category: current.filter(c => c !== cat) }; return { ...prev, category: [...current, cat] }; }); };
    const handleDelete = async () => { openConfirm("정말 이 일정을 삭제하시겠습니까?", async () => { const res = await operations.deleteTask(selectedItems.task.id, selectedItems.task.topic, syncGroup ? selectedItems.task.groupId : null); if(res) { showToast("삭제되었습니다."); setMode('list'); } else { showToast("삭제 실패", 'error'); } }); };

    return (<div className="fixed inset-0 z-[110] flex items-center justify-center bg-[#3a2d20]/30 backdrop-blur-sm p-4"><div className="bg-[#faf6ef] w-full max-w-xl rounded-2xl shadow-2xl flex flex-col max-h-[85vh]"><div className="p-4 border-b border-[#e8dcc8] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#faf6ef]/50 rounded-t-2xl"><div><h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-[#42392e] flex items-center gap-2">{mode === 'list' ? (selectedDate ? `${selectedDate} 일정` : '일정 관리') : (mode === 'create' ? '새 일정 추가' : '일정 수정')}</h2><p className="text-xs text-[#6a5d50]">{mode === 'list' ? `총 ${dailyTasks.length}개의 일정이 있습니다` : (tab === 'work' ? '업무 추가/수정' : '개인 일정 추가/수정')}</p></div><button onClick={()=>toggleModal('schedule', false)}><X size={20} className="text-[#857460] hover:text-[#5a4d40]"/></button></div><div className="p-5 overflow-y-auto flex-1 custom-scrollbar">{mode === 'list' ? (<div className="flex flex-col h-full"><div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto space-y-2 min-h-[200px] mb-4">{dailyTasks.length > 0 ? (dailyTasks.map(task => { const linkedPlan = plans.find(p => p.id === task.planId); const isPersonal = task.type === 'personal'; let borderClass = "border-[#d4c4ac] hover:border-[#5d6a7a]"; let bgClass = "bg-[#faf6ef]"; let iconColor = "text-[#857460]"; if (isPersonal) { bgClass = "bg-[#7a5d6a]/10/50"; borderClass = "border-[#7a5d6a]/30 hover:border-[#7a5d6a]/50"; iconColor = "text-[#7a5d6a]"; } else if (linkedPlan?.type === 'shorts') { bgClass = "bg-[#b8860b]/10/50"; borderClass = "border-[#b8860b]/30 hover:border-[#b8860b]/50"; iconColor = "text-[#b8860b]"; } return (<div key={task.id} onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); }} className={`p-3 rounded-xl border ${borderClass} ${bgClass} cursor-pointer transition-all shadow-sm group`}><div className="flex items-start gap-3"><div className={`mt-0.5 ${task.status === 'done' ? 'text-[#5d7a5d]' : iconColor}`}>{task.status === 'done' ? <CheckCircle size={18} className="fill-[#5d7a5d]/30"/> : (isPersonal ? <User size={18}/> : <Film size={18}/>)}</div><div className="flex-1 min-w-0"><div className={`text-sm font-bold ${task.status === 'done' ? 'text-[#857460] line-through' : 'text-[#42392e]'}`}>{task.details || '내용 없음'}</div><div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">{!isPersonal && linkedPlan && (<span className="text-[10px] bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[#6a5d50] truncate max-w-[150px]">{linkedPlan.topic}</span>)}<span className="text-[10px] text-[#857460] flex items-center gap-1"><User size={10}/> {task.author}</span>{task.category?.map(c => (<span key={c} className="text-[10px] text-[#857460]">#{c}</span>))}</div></div><div className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"><Edit size={14} className="text-[#857460]"/></div></div></div>); })) : (<div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-[#857460] border-2 border-dashed border-[#e8dcc8] rounded-xl bg-[#faf6ef]/50 py-10"><ClipboardList size={32} className="mb-2 opacity-50"/><div className="text-xs">등록된 일정이 없습니다</div></div>)}</div><div className="pt-4 border-t border-[#e8dcc8]"><label className="text-xs font-bold text-[#857460] block mb-2 text-center uppercase">새 일정 추가</label><div className="flex gap-2"><button onClick={() => handleCreate('task')} className="flex-1 py-3 bg-[#5d6a7a]/10 text-[#4d5a6a] font-bold rounded-xl hover:bg-[#5d6a7a]/20 hover:scale-[1.02] transition-all text-sm flex items-center justify-center gap-2 shadow-sm"><Briefcase size={16}/> 업무 일정 등록</button><button onClick={() => handleCreate('personal')} className="flex-1 py-3 bg-[#7a5d6a]/10 text-[#6a4d5a] font-bold rounded-xl hover:bg-[#7a5d6a]/20 hover:scale-[1.02] transition-all text-sm flex items-center justify-center gap-2 shadow-sm"><Coffee size={16}/> 개인 일정 등록</button></div></div></div>) : (<div className="space-y-4"><div className="flex p-1 bg-[#f5f0e6] rounded-xl mb-4"><button onClick={() => { setTab('work'); setFormData({...formData, type: 'task'}); }} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded-lg transition-all ${tab === 'work' ? 'bg-[#faf6ef] shadow text-[#4d5a6a]' : 'text-[#857460]'}`}>업무 (Project)</button><button onClick={() => { setTab('personal'); setFormData({...formData, type: 'personal'}); }} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded-lg transition-all ${tab === 'personal' ? 'bg-[#faf6ef] shadow text-[#6a4d5a]' : 'text-[#857460]'}`}>개인 일정 (Personal)</button></div><div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3"><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">담당자</label><input value={formData.author || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, author: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-2.5 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] text-[#32291e]" placeholder="이름 입력"/></div></div>{tab === 'work' && (<div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">연결된 프로젝트</label><select value={formData.planId || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, planId: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-2.5 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] text-[#32291e]"><option value="" disabled>프로젝트 선택</option><optgroup label="진행 중">{plans.filter(p => p.status === 'active').map(p => <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>[{PROJECT_TYPES[p.type || 'main']?.label}] {p.topic}</option>)}</optgroup><optgroup label="기획 대기">{plans.filter(p => p.status === 'draft').map(p => <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>[{PROJECT_TYPES[p.type || 'main']?.label}] {p.topic} (기획중)</option>)}</optgroup></select></div>)}<div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">{tab === 'work' ? '업무 상세 내용' : '일정 내용 (사유 등)'}</label><textarea value={formData.details || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, details: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm h-24 resize-none focus:outline-none focus:border-[#5d6a7a] text-[#32291e]" placeholder={tab === 'work' ? "업무 내용을 입력하세요" : "예: 병원 진료, 개인 사정 등"}/></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">분류</label><div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">{tab === 'work' ? (Object.keys(WORK_CATEGORIES).map(cat => {const isActive = (formData.category || []).includes(cat); return (<button key={cat} onClick={() => toggleCategory(cat)} className={`px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-bold rounded-lg border transition-all ${isActive ? WORK_CATEGORIES[cat].color : 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#d4c4ac] text-[#6a5d50]'}`}>{cat}</button>) })) : (Object.keys(PERSONAL_CATEGORIES).map(cat => {const isActive = (formData.category || []).includes(cat); return (<button key={cat} onClick={() => toggleCategory(cat, true)} className={`px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-bold rounded-lg border transition-all ${isActive ? PERSONAL_CATEGORIES[cat].color : 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#d4c4ac] text-[#6a5d50]'}`}>{cat}</button>) }))}</div></div><div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3"><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">시작일</label><input type="date" value={formData.workStartDate || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, workStartDate: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-2 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]"/></div><div><label className="block text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] mb-1">종료일</label><input type="date" value={formData.workEndDate || ''} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, workEndDate: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-2 bg-[#faf6ef] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg text-sm text-[#32291e]"/></div></div>{mode === 'edit' && tab === 'work' && formData.id && (<div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-[#5d7a5d]/10 rounded-xl border border-[#5d7a5d]/30"><div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-3"><span className="text-xs font-bold text-[#3d5a3d] flex items-center gap-1"><CheckSquare size={14}/> 일일 업무 완료 체크</span><span className="text-[10px] text-[#4d6a4d] font-bold bg-[#faf6ef] px-2 py-1 rounded-full border border-[#5d7a5d]/30">{(formData.completedDates || []).length} / {dateRange.length} 완료</span></div><div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 max-h-[150px] overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">{dateRange.map(date => { const isDone = (formData.completedDates || []).includes(date); const isToday = date === formatDateLocal(new Date()); const isOff = isHolidayOrWeekend(date); return (<button key={date} onClick={() => toggleDateCompletion(date)} className={`px-2 py-2 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition-all flex flex-col items-center gap-1 ${isDone ? 'bg-[#5d7a5d] text-[#faf6ef] border-[#4d6a4d] shadow-md' : (isToday ? 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#5d6a7a]/50 text-[#4a3d30] ring-1 ring-[#5d6a7a]/40' : 'bg-[#faf6ef] border-[#5d7a5d]/30 text-[#6a5d50] hover:border-emerald-300')} ${isOff && !isDone ? 'opacity-60 bg-[#faf6ef]' : ''}`} title={isOff ? "휴일/주말" : ""}><span className={isDone ? 'text-emerald-100' : (isOff ? 'text-red-300' : 'text-[#857460]')}>{date.slice(5)}</span>{isDone ? <CheckCircle size={14}/> : <div className="w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full border-2 border-[#d4c4ac]"/>}</button>); })}</div>{dateRange.length === 0 && <div className="text-center text-xs text-[#857460] py-2">설정된 날짜 범위가 없습니다.</div>}</div>)}<div className="flex flex-col gap-2 pt-2 border-t border-[#f5f0e6] mt-2">{mode === 'edit' && formData.groupId && (<button onClick={() => setSyncGroup(!syncGroup)} className={`flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-bold px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition-all ${syncGroup ? 'bg-[#6a5d7a]/10 text-[#4a3d5a] border border-[#6a5d7a]/30' : 'bg-[#faf6ef] text-[#6a5d50] border border-[#d4c4ac]'}`}><Link size={14} className={syncGroup ? "text-[#5a4d6a]" : "text-[#857460]"} /> {syncGroup ? '🔗 연결된 모든 날짜 일정 변경 (권장)' : '🔓 이 날짜의 일정만 독립적으로 변경'}</button>)}{mode === 'edit' && (<button onClick={handleDelete} className="w-full mt-2 py-2 text-[#9b4d4d] hover:bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold border border-transparent hover:border-[#9b4d4d]/30 transition-colors"><Trash size={14} className="inline mr-1"/> 일정 삭제</button>)}</div></div>)}</div><div className="p-4 border-t border-[#e8dcc8] bg-[#faf6ef]/50 rounded-b-2xl flex justify-end gap-2">{mode === 'list' ? (<button onClick={()=>toggleModal('schedule', false)} className="px-5 py-2 bg-[#e8dcc8] text-[#5a4d40] font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-[#d4c4ac]">닫기</button>) : (<><button onClick={() => setMode('list')} className="px-4 py-2 text-[#6a5d50] font-bold hover:bg-[#e8dcc8] rounded-lg">취소</button><button onClick={handleSaveInternal} disabled={isSaving} className={`px-6 py-2 text-[#faf6ef] font-bold rounded-lg shadow-md transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50 ${tab === 'personal' ? 'bg-[#6a4d5a] hover:bg-[#5a3d4a]' : 'bg-[#4d5a6a] hover:bg-[#3d4a5a]'}`}>{isSaving && <Loader size={14} className="animate-spin"/>}{isSaving ? '저장 중...' : '저장'}</button></>)}</div></div></div>);
};

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 8. View Components
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// [최적화] PlanCard Memoization
const PlanCard = React.memo(({ plan, tasks, operations, onClick, onTaskStatusChange }) => {
    const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);
    const summary = useMemo(() => {
        const realTasks = tasks.filter(t => !t.isDraftPlaceholder && t.type !== 'personal');
        let totalDays = 0; let completedDaysCount = 0;
        realTasks.forEach(t => { const start = parseLocalDate(t.workStartDate); const end = parseLocalDate(t.workEndDate); const duration = Math.floor((end - start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) + 1; if (duration > 0) totalDays += duration; if (t.completedDates && Array.isArray(t.completedDates)) { completedDaysCount += t.completedDates.length; } });
        const progress = totalDays === 0 ? 0 : Math.min(100, Math.round((completedDaysCount / totalDays) * 100));
        const pendingTasks = realTasks.filter(t => t.status !== 'done'); let nextDue = null;
        if (pendingTasks.length > 0) { const sorted = [...pendingTasks].sort((a, b) => new Date(a.workEndDate) - new Date(b.workEndDate)); nextDue = sorted[0].workEndDate; }
        return { total: realTasks.length, progress, nextDue, realTasks };
    }, [tasks]);
    const handleTaskCheck = (e, task) => { e.stopPropagation(); const newStatus = task.status === 'done' ? 'in_progress' : 'done'; onTaskStatusChange(task, newStatus); };
    const isShorts = plan.type === 'shorts';
    return (
        <div className={`bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-xl border transition-all duration-200 shadow-sm hover:shadow-md ${isExpanded ? 'ring-2 ring-[#5d6a7a]/30 border-[#5d6a7a]/50' : 'border-[#d4c4ac]'}`}>
            <div className="p-4 cursor-pointer" onClick={() => setIsExpanded(!isExpanded)}><div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><span className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold ${isShorts ? 'bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 text-[#8b3d3d]' : 'bg-[#6a5d7a]/10 text-[#5a4d6a]'}`}>{isShorts ? 'Shorts' : 'Main'}</span>{plan.status === 'active' && (<div className="flex items-center gap-1"><span className="text-xs font-bold text-[#4d5a6a]">{summary.progress}%</span><div className="w-10 h-1.5 bg-[#f5f0e6] rounded-full overflow-hidden"><div className="h-full bg-[#5d6a7a] transition-all duration-500" style={{ width: `${summary.progress}%` }} /></div></div>)}</div><h4 className="font-bold text-[#42392e] text-sm mb-1 line-clamp-2 leading-snug">{plan.topic}</h4><div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-2"><span className="text-xs text-[#6a5d50] flex items-center gap-1"><User size={12} /> {plan.planner}</span>{summary.nextDue && (<span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#9b4d4d] bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded flex items-center gap-1"><CalendarIcon size={10} /> ~{summary.nextDue.slice(5)}</span>)}</div></div>
            {isExpanded && (<div className="px-4 pb-4 pt-0 border-t border-[#f5f0e6] bg-[#faf6ef]/50 rounded-b-xl animate-in slide-in-from-top-2 duration-200"><div className="mt-3 space-y-2">{summary.realTasks.length > 0 ? (summary.realTasks.map(task => { const completedCount = task.completedDates ? task.completedDates.length : 0; const start = parseLocalDate(task.workStartDate); const end = parseLocalDate(task.workEndDate); const totalDays = Math.floor((end - start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) + 1; const percent = totalDays > 0 ? Math.round((completedCount / totalDays) * 100) : 0; return (<div key={task.id} className="flex flex-col gap-1 p-2 bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-lg border border-[#e8dcc8] hover:border-[#5d6a7a]/40 transition-colors"><div className="flex items-center gap-2"><button onClick={(e) => handleTaskCheck(e, task)} className={`p-1 rounded-full transition-colors ${task.status === 'done' ? 'text-[#5d7a5d] bg-[#5d7a5d]/10' : 'text-slate-300 hover:text-[#5d6a7a]'}`}><CheckCircle size={16} className={task.status === 'done' ? 'fill-emerald-500 text-[#faf6ef]' : ''} /></button><div className="flex-1 min-w-0" onClick={() => onClick(task)}><div className={`text-xs font-medium truncate cursor-pointer ${task.status === 'done' ? 'text-[#857460] line-through' : 'text-[#4a3d30]'}`}>{task.details || '상세 내용 없음'}</div><div className="text-[10px] text-[#857460] flex gap-2"><span>{task.author}</span><span>{task.category?.join(', ')}</span></div></div></div><div className="w-full bg-[#f5f0e6] h-1 rounded-full overflow-hidden mt-1"><div className="bg-[#5d6a7a] h-full" style={{ width: `${percent}%` }}></div></div></div>) })) : (<div className="text-center py-4 text-xs text-[#857460]">{plan.status === 'draft' ? '기획 승인 후 일정이 생성됩니다.' : '등록된 상세 업무가 없습니다.'}</div>)}<div className="flex justify-end gap-2 mt-3 pt-2 border-t border-[#e8dcc8]"><button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onClick(null, plan); }} className="text-xs font-bold text-[#6a5d50] hover:text-[#4d5a6a] px-2 py-1">기획안 보기</button>{plan.status === 'active' && (<button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onClick({ planId: plan.id, status: 'in_progress', type: 'task' }); }} className="text-xs font-bold bg-[#5d6a7a]/20 text-[#4d5a6a] px-3 py-1 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-200">+ 업무 추가</button>)}</div></div></div>)}
        </div>
    );
}, (prev, next) => {
    return prev.plan.id === next.plan.id && 
           prev.plan.status === next.plan.status && 
           prev.tasks.length === next.tasks.length &&
           prev.tasks.every((t, i) => t.id === next.tasks[i]?.id && t.status === next.tasks[i]?.status && t.completedDates?.length === next.tasks[i]?.completedDates?.length);
});

// [New] 업무 타입 기반 색상 결정 함수
const getTaskColorByCategory = (task, linkedPlan) => {
    // 개인 일정
    if (task.type === 'personal') {
        return {
            bg: 'bg-amber-900/40',
            text: 'text-[#a0714a]',
            border: 'border-[#a0714a]/40'
        };
    }
    
    // 완료된 프로젝트는 회색 처리
    if (linkedPlan?.status === 'completed') {
        return {
            bg: 'bg-[#44403c]',
            text: 'text-[#a89880]',
            border: 'border-[#57534e]',
            completed: true
        };
    }
    
    // 업무 카테고리별 색상 정의
    const CATEGORY_COLORS = {
        '대본': {
            bg: 'bg-blue-900/40',
            text: 'text-blue-300',
            border: 'border-[#5d6a7a]/40'
        },
        '촬영': {
            bg: 'bg-orange-900/40',
            text: 'text-orange-300',
            border: 'border-orange-500/40'
        },
        '편집': {
            bg: 'bg-emerald-900/40',
            text: 'text-emerald-300',
            border: 'border-[#5d7a5d]/40'
        },
        '업데이트': {
            bg: 'bg-purple-900/40',
            text: 'text-purple-300',
            border: 'border-purple-500/40'
        }
    };
    
    // 첫 번째 카테고리 기준으로 색상 결정
    const primaryCategory = task.category?.[0];
    
    if (primaryCategory && CATEGORY_COLORS[primaryCategory]) {
        return CATEGORY_COLORS[primaryCategory];
    }
    
    // 카테고리 없으면 기본 색상
    return {
        bg: 'bg-[#4a3d30]/40',
        text: 'text-slate-300',
        border: 'border-[#f5f0e6]0/40'
    };
};

// [최적화] TaskBar Memoization
// planId로 plans를 탐색하는 과정을 useMemo로 최적화
const TaskBar = React.memo(({ task, plans, isPersonal, onClick }) => {
    const linkedPlan = useMemo(() => 
        isPersonal ? null : plans.find(p => p.id === task.planId), 
        [isPersonal, plans, task.planId]
    );
    
    // ✅ 새로운 색상 시스템 적용
    const colorScheme = useMemo(() => 
        getTaskColorByCategory(task, linkedPlan), 
        [task, linkedPlan]
    );
    
    const isCompleted = colorScheme.completed || false;
    
    // 아이콘 결정 (업무 타입별)
    let IconComp = null;
    if (isPersonal) {
        const cat = task.category?.[0];
        IconComp = PERSONAL_CATEGORIES[cat]?.icon;
    } else {
        const primaryCategory = task.category?.[0];
        IconComp = WORK_CATEGORIES[primaryCategory]?.icon || FileText;
    }
    
    // 최종 클래스 조합
    const finalClasses = isCompleted
        ? `${colorScheme.bg} ${colorScheme.text} border ${colorScheme.border} line-through decoration-[#78716c] opacity-60`
        : `${colorScheme.bg} ${colorScheme.text} border ${colorScheme.border}`;
    
    // [New] 진행률 계산 로직
    const totalWorkDays = getDaysDifference(task.workStartDate, task.workEndDate) + 1;
    const getProgress = () => {
        if (task.status === 'done') return 100;
        if (!task.completedDates || task.completedDates.length === 0) return 0;
        if (totalWorkDays <= 0) return 0;
        return Math.round((task.completedDates.length / totalWorkDays) * 100);
    };
    const progress = getProgress();
    
    return (
        <div 
            draggable 
            onDragStart={(e) => {
                e.dataTransfer.setData('taskId', task.id);
                e.dataTransfer.setData('source', 'calendar');
                e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
            }} 
            onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                onClick(task);
            }} 
            className={`relative group p-1.5 rounded text-xs font-bold truncate flex items-center gap-1 shadow-sm cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:brightness-110 transition-all ${finalClasses}`} 
            title={task.details}
        >
            {/* 담당자 이니셜 */}
            <span className="font-black opacity-50 mr-0.5 text-[9px]">
                {task.author?.[0] || '?'}
            </span>
            
            {/* 업무 타입 아이콘 */}
            {IconComp && <IconComp size={8} className="opacity-70"/>}
            
            {/* 프로젝트명 또는 카테고리 + 업무내용 */}
            <span className="truncate">
                {isPersonal 
                    ? (task.details || task.category?.[0] || '개인') 
                    : (task.details || task.topic || '업무')
                }
            </span>

            {/* 하단 진행 바 */}
            <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 h-1 bg-[#42392e]/20 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity rounded-b overflow-hidden">
                <div 
                    className={`h-full rounded-b transition-all ${
                        progress === 100 ? 'bg-[#5d7a5d]' : 
                        progress > 0 ? 'bg-[#5d6a7a]' : 
                        'bg-[#6a5d50]'
                    }`}
                    style={{ width: `${progress}%` }}
                />
            </div>

            {/* 완료 체크 마크 */}
            {task.status === 'done' && (
                <CheckCircle 
                    size={12} 
                    className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 text-[#5d7a5d] bg-emerald-900 rounded-full fill-emerald-400 shadow-sm z-10"
                />
            )}

            {/* 툴팁 */}
            <div className="absolute bottom-full left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 mb-2 px-2 py-1 bg-black/90 text-[#faf6ef] text-[10px] rounded opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity pointer-events-none whitespace-nowrap z-50 shadow-lg">
                {task.author} • {progress}% 완료 ({task.completedDates?.length || 0}/{totalWorkDays}일)
            </div>
        </div>
    );
}, (prev, next) => {
    return prev.task.id === next.task.id && 
           prev.task.status === next.task.status && 
           prev.task.category?.[0] === next.task.category?.[0] &&
           prev.task.workStartDate === next.task.workStartDate &&
           prev.task.workEndDate === next.task.workEndDate &&
           prev.task.completedDates?.length === next.task.completedDates?.length && // [New] 진행률 변경 감지
           prev.plans.length === next.plans.length; 
});

const MonthView = () => {
    const { currentDate, tasksByDate, filteredTasks, plans, toggleModal, setSelectedItems, setSelectedDate, operations } = useApp();
    const getCalendarDays = (date) => { const year = date.getFullYear(); const month = date.getMonth(); const startDate = new Date(year, month, 1); startDate.setDate(1 - startDate.getDay()); const days = []; for (let i = 0; i < 42; i++) { const d = new Date(startDate); d.setDate(startDate.getDate() + i); days.push({ date: d, isCurrentMonth: d.getMonth() === month }); } return days; };
    const calendarDays = useMemo(() => getCalendarDays(currentDate), [currentDate]);
    const handleDrop = async (e, dateStr) => { e.preventDefault(); const taskId = e.dataTransfer.getData('taskId'); if (taskId) { const task = filteredTasks.find(t => t.id === taskId); if (task) await operations.moveTask(task, dateStr); } };
    return (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-px bg-[#d4c4ac] border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
            {/* 요일 헤더 */}
            {['SUN', 'MON', 'TUE', 'WED', 'THU', 'FRI', 'SAT'].map((day, i) => (
                <div key={day} className={`bg-[#f0e9de] py-3 text-center text-xs font-bold ${i === 0 ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : 'text-[#a89880]'}`}>{day}</div>
            ))}
            {/* 날짜 셀 */}
            {calendarDays.map((dayObj, idx) => { 
                const dateStr = formatDateLocal(dayObj.date); 
                const isToday = formatDateLocal(new Date()) === dateStr; 
                const holidayName = HOLIDAYS[dateStr]; 
                const dayTasks = tasksByDate[dateStr] || []; 
                return (
                    <div 
                        key={idx} 
                        onDragOver={(e) => e.preventDefault()} 
                        onDrop={(e) => handleDrop(e, dateStr)} 
                        onClick={() => { setSelectedDate(dateStr); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task: null})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} 
                        className={`bg-[#faf6ef] h-[120px] p-2 hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] transition-colors cursor-pointer relative group flex flex-col ${!dayObj.isCurrentMonth ? 'opacity-30 bg-[#f0e9de]' : ''}`}
                    >
                        {/* 날짜 헤더 */}
                        <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-1 flex-shrink-0">
                            <div className={`text-sm font-bold w-7 h-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full ${isToday ? 'bg-[#a0714a] text-[#faf6ef]' : (holidayName || dayObj.date.getDay() === 0 ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : 'text-[#42392e]')}`}>
                                {dayObj.date.getDate()}
                            </div>
                            {holidayName && <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-[#9b4d4d] bg-[#9b4d4d]/10 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded truncate max-w-[70px]">{holidayName}</span>}
                        </div>
                        {/* 업무 목록 */}
                        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col gap-0.5 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar min-h-0">
                            {dayTasks.slice(0, 4).map(t => (
                                <TaskBar key={t.id} task={t} plans={plans} isPersonal={t.type === 'personal'} onClick={(task) => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} />
                            ))}
                            {dayTasks.length > 4 && (
                                <div className="text-[9px] text-[#857460] text-center py-0.5 bg-[#f0e9de] rounded">+{dayTasks.length - 4}개 더보기</div>
                            )}
                        </div>
                        {/* 추가 버튼 */}
                        <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                            <Plus size={14} className="text-[#a0714a]"/>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                ); 
            })}
        </div>
    );
};

const WeekView = () => {
    const { currentDate, tasksByDate, filteredTasks, plans, toggleModal, setSelectedItems, setSelectedDate, operations } = useApp();
    const weekDays = useMemo(() => getWeekDays(currentDate), [currentDate]);
    const handleDrop = async (e, dateStr) => { e.preventDefault(); const taskId = e.dataTransfer.getData('taskId'); if (taskId) { const task = filteredTasks.find(t => t.id === taskId); if(task) await operations.moveTask(task, dateStr); } };
    return (<div className="flex h-full border border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-lg overflow-hidden vj-card bg-[#faf6ef]">{weekDays.map((day, i) => { const dateStr = formatDateLocal(day); const isToday = formatDateLocal(new Date()) === dateStr; const holidayName = HOLIDAYS[dateStr]; const dayTasks = tasksByDate[dateStr] || []; return (<div key={dateStr} onDragOver={(e) => e.preventDefault()} onDrop={(e) => handleDrop(e, dateStr)} onClick={() => { setSelectedDate(dateStr); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task: null})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} className="flex-1 border-r border-[#d4c4ac] last:border-0 flex flex-col min-w-[100px] group hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] transition-colors"><div className={`p-3 text-center border-b border-[#d4c4ac] ${isToday ? 'bg-[#f5f0e6]' : 'bg-[#f0e9de]'}`}><div className={`text-xs font-bold mb-1 ${i === 0 ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : 'text-[#a89880]'}`}>{['일','월','화','수','목','금','토'][day.getDay()]}</div><div className={`text-lg font-black ${isToday ? 'text-[#a0714a]' : (i===0 ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : 'text-[#42392e]')}`}>{day.getDate()}</div>{holidayName && <div className="text-[10px] text-[#9b4d4d] mt-1 truncate">{holidayName}</div>}</div><div className="flex-1 p-2 space-y-2 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar relative">{dayTasks.map(t => (<TaskBar key={t.id} task={t} plans={plans} isPersonal={t.type === 'personal'} onClick={(task) => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} />))}<div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-10 pointer-events-none"><Plus className="text-[#44403c]" size={24}/></div></div></div>); })}</div>);
};

const KanbanView = () => {
    const { plans, filteredTasks, toggleModal, setSelectedItems, operations, showToast } = useApp();
    const aggregatedPlans = useMemo(() => { const grouped = {}; plans.forEach(plan => { grouped[plan.id] = { plan: plan, tasks: [] }; }); filteredTasks.forEach(task => { if (task.planId && grouped[task.planId]) { grouped[task.planId].tasks.push(task); } }); return Object.values(grouped); }, [plans, filteredTasks]);
    const handleTaskStatusChange = useCallback(async (task, newStatus) => { const result = await operations.saveTask({ ...task, status: newStatus }, true, false, false); if (result.success) { showToast('업무 상태가 변경되었습니다.'); } }, [operations, showToast]);
    const handleItemClick = useCallback((task, plan = null) => { if (task) { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); } else if (plan) { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, plan})); toggleModal('plan', true); } }, [setSelectedItems, toggleModal]);
    return (<div className="flex gap-4 h-full overflow-x-auto pb-4 px-2">{Object.entries(PLAN_COLUMNS).map(([statusKey, config]) => { const columnItems = aggregatedPlans.filter(item => item.plan.status === statusKey); return (<div key={statusKey} className="flex-1 min-w-[320px] max-w-[400px] flex flex-col h-full bg-[#f0e9de] rounded-2xl border border-[#d4c4ac]"><div className={`p-4 rounded-t-2xl border-b border-[#d4c4ac] flex justify-between items-center vj-card bg-[#faf6ef]`}><h3 className={`font-black text-sm flex items-center gap-2 text-[#42392e]`}>{statusKey === 'draft' ? <StickyNote size={18} className="text-[#857460]"/> : (statusKey === 'active' ? <Activity size={18} className="text-[#a0714a]"/> : <CheckCircle size={18} className="text-[#5d7a5d]"/>)}{config.label}</h3><span className="bg-[#44403c] text-[#857460] px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-bold">{columnItems.length}</span></div><div className="flex-1 p-4 space-y-4 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">{columnItems.length > 0 ? (columnItems.map(({ plan, tasks }) => (<PlanCard key={plan.id} plan={plan} tasks={tasks} operations={operations} onClick={handleItemClick} onTaskStatusChange={handleTaskStatusChange}/>))) : (<div className="h-32 flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-[#44403c] border-2 border-dashed border-[#d4c4ac] rounded-xl vj-card bg-[#faf6ef]/30"><ClipboardList size={24} className="mb-2 opacity-50"/><span className="text-xs font-bold">프로젝트 없음</span></div>)}</div></div>); })}</div>);
};

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------
// 9. Tab Components
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------

// 📋 대시보드 탭 (신규)
const DashboardTab = () => {
    const { profile, plans, filteredTasks, managements, logs, toggleModal, setSelectedItems, setSelectedDate } = useApp();
    const today = formatDateLocal(new Date());
    const [selectedStatus, setSelectedStatus] = useState(null);

    // 이번 주 7일
    const weekDays = useMemo(() => getWeekDays(new Date()), []);

    // 내 일정만 (로그인 유저)
    const myTasks = useMemo(() => filteredTasks.filter(t => !t.isDraftPlaceholder && t.author === profile), [filteredTasks, profile]);

    // 날짜별 내 태스크
    const myTasksByDate = useMemo(() => {
        const map = {};
        weekDays.forEach(day => {
            const dateStr = formatDateLocal(day);
            map[dateStr] = myTasks.filter(t => t.workStartDate <= dateStr && t.workEndDate >= dateStr);
        });
        return map;
    }, [myTasks, weekDays]);

    // 이번 주 전체 업무
    const weekTasks = useMemo(() => {
        const weekStartStr = formatDateLocal(weekDays[0]);
        const weekEndStr = formatDateLocal(weekDays[6]);
        return filteredTasks.filter(t => {
            if (t.isDraftPlaceholder) return false;
            return t.workStartDate <= weekEndStr && t.workEndDate >= weekStartStr;
        });
    }, [filteredTasks, weekDays]);

    const weekSummary = useMemo(() => ({
        total: weekTasks.length,
        done: weekTasks.filter(t => t.status === 'done').length,
        inProgress: weekTasks.filter(t => t.status === 'in_progress').length,
        todo: weekTasks.filter(t => t.status === 'todo').length
    }), [weekTasks]);

    const selectedTasks = useMemo(() => {
        if (!selectedStatus) return [];
        if (selectedStatus === 'all') return weekTasks;
        return weekTasks.filter(t => t.status === selectedStatus);
    }, [selectedStatus, weekTasks]);

    // 오늘 할 일
    const todayTasks = useMemo(() => filteredTasks.filter(t =>
        !t.isDraftPlaceholder && t.workStartDate <= today && t.workEndDate >= today && t.status !== 'done'
    ).slice(0, 5), [filteredTasks, today]);

    // 진행중 프로젝트 TOP 3
    const activeProjects = useMemo(() => plans.filter(p => p.status === 'active').map(plan => {
        const planTasks = filteredTasks.filter(t => t.planId === plan.id && !t.isDraftPlaceholder);
        let totalDays = 0, completedDays = 0;
        planTasks.forEach(t => {
            const start = parseLocalDate(t.workStartDate);
            const end = parseLocalDate(t.workEndDate);
            const duration = Math.floor((end - start) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) + 1;
            if (duration > 0) totalDays += duration;
            if (t.completedDates) completedDays += t.completedDates.length;
        });
        return { ...plan, progress: totalDays === 0 ? 0 : Math.min(100, Math.round((completedDays / totalDays) * 100)) };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.progress - a.progress).slice(0, 3), [plans, filteredTasks]);

    // 팀원별 현황
    const teamStatus = useMemo(() => TEAM_MEMBERS.map(member => {
        const memberTasks = filteredTasks.filter(t =>
            t.author === member && !t.isDraftPlaceholder && t.workStartDate <= today && t.workEndDate >= today
        );
        const doing = memberTasks.find(t => t.status === 'in_progress');
        return { name: member, taskCount: memberTasks.length, currentTask: doing?.details || (memberTasks[0]?.details || '예정된 업무 없음') };
    }), [filteredTasks, today]);

    const recentLogs = useMemo(() => logs.slice(0, 5), [logs]);

    const financeSummary = useMemo(() => {
        const thisMonth = new Date();
        const monthItems = managements.filter(m => m.category === 'finance' && m.datetime && (() => {
            const d = new Date(m.datetime);
            return d.getMonth() === thisMonth.getMonth() && d.getFullYear() === thisMonth.getFullYear();
        })());
        const income = monthItems.filter(i => i.type === 'income').reduce((sum, i) => sum + (Number(i.amount) || 0), 0);
        const expense = monthItems.filter(i => i.type === 'expense').reduce((sum, i) => sum + (Number(i.amount) || 0), 0);
        return { income, expense, balance: income - expense };
    }, [managements]);

    const statusCards = [
        { key: 'all', label: '이번 주 전체', count: weekSummary.total, unit: '개의 업무', activeColor: 'border-[#a0714a] ring-2 ring-[#a0714a]/30', countColor: 'text-[#42392e]', badgeColor: 'bg-[#a0714a] text-[#faf6ef]' },
        { key: 'done', label: '완료', count: weekSummary.done, unit: '개 완료', activeColor: 'border-[#5d7a5d] ring-2 ring-[#5d7a5d]/30', countColor: 'text-[#5d7a5d]', badgeColor: 'bg-[#5d7a5d] text-[#faf6ef]' },
        { key: 'in_progress', label: '진행중', count: weekSummary.inProgress, unit: '개 진행중', activeColor: 'border-[#a0714a] ring-2 ring-[#a0714a]/30', countColor: 'text-[#a0714a]', badgeColor: 'bg-[#a0714a] text-[#faf6ef]' },
        { key: 'todo', label: '대기', count: weekSummary.todo, unit: '개 대기', activeColor: 'border-[#857460] ring-2 ring-[#857460]/30', countColor: 'text-[#857460]', badgeColor: 'bg-[#857460] text-[#faf6ef]' },
    ];
    const statusLabel = { all: '이번 주 전체', done: '완료', in_progress: '진행중', todo: '대기' };

    // 타임라인 태스크 색상 + 이모지
    const getBarStyle = (task) => {
        if (task.type === 'personal') {
            const cat = task.category?.[0];
            const personalEmoji = { '연차': '🏖️', '오전반차': '🌅', '오후반차': '🌇', '외근': '🗺️', '미팅': '🤝', '기타': '🙂' };
            return { bg: 'bg-amber-900/30 border-[#a0714a]/40', text: 'text-[#6a4a2a]', emoji: personalEmoji[cat] || '👤' };
        }
        const cat = task.category?.[0];
        const styles = {
            '대본': { bg: 'bg-blue-900/30 border-[#5d6a7a]/40', text: 'text-[#2d3d4a]', emoji: '📝' },
            '촬영': { bg: 'bg-orange-900/30 border-orange-500/40', text: 'text-[#5a3000]', emoji: '🎥' },
            '편집': { bg: 'bg-emerald-900/30 border-[#5d7a5d]/40', text: 'text-[#1d4a1d]', emoji: '✂️' },
            '업데이트': { bg: 'bg-purple-900/30 border-purple-500/40', text: 'text-[#3a1d5a]', emoji: '🔄' },
        };
        return styles[cat] || { bg: 'bg-[#857460]/20 border-[#857460]/40', text: 'text-[#4a3d30]', emoji: '📋' };
    };

    const DAY_NAMES_KR = ['SUN', 'MON', 'TUE', 'WED', 'THU', 'FRI', 'SAT'];

    return (
        <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* 인사 + 타임라인 카드 */}
            <div className="vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl p-6 border border-[#d4c4ac]">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5">
                    <div>
                        <h2 className="text-2xl font-black text-[#42392e]">안녕하세요, {profile}님 👋</h2>
                        <p className="text-sm text-[#857460] mt-1">
                            {new Date().toLocaleDateString('ko-KR', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'long' })} · 이번 주 업무 현황입니다
                        </p>
                    </div>
                    <button
                        onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedDate(today);
                            setSelectedItems(prev => ({
                                ...prev,
                                task: { type: 'personal', author: profile, category: ['기타'], workStartDate: today, workEndDate: today, status: 'todo', completedDates: [] }
                            }));
                            toggleModal('schedule', true);
                        }}
                        className="px-4 py-2.5 bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] text-[#42392e] font-bold rounded-xl text-sm flex items-center gap-2 hover:bg-[#e8dcc8] transition-all"
                    >
                        <Plus size={16}/> 🙂 개인 일정 추가
                    </button>
                </div>

                {/* 타임라인 레이블 */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                    <span className="text-xs font-bold text-[#a0714a]">📅 이번 주 내 일정 타임라인</span>
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-[#a89880]">빈 칸 클릭 → 빠른 등록 · 항목 클릭 → 수정</span>
                    {/* 범례 */}
                    <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-3">
                        {[['📝','대본'], ['🎥','촬영'], ['✂️','편집'], ['🔄','업데이트'], ['👤','개인']].map(([emoji, label]) => (
                            <span key={label} className="text-[10px] text-[#a89880] flex items-center gap-1">{emoji} {label}</span>
                        ))}
                    </div>
                </div>

                {/* 7일 그리드 */}
                <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2">
                    {weekDays.map((day, i) => {
                        const dateStr = formatDateLocal(day);
                        const isToday = dateStr === today;
                        const dayTasks = myTasksByDate[dateStr] || [];
                        const isWeekend = i === 0 || i === 6;
                        const holidayName = HOLIDAYS[dateStr];

                        return (
                            <div key={dateStr} className={`rounded-xl border overflow-hidden flex flex-col transition-all ${isToday ? 'border-[#a0714a] border-2 shadow-md' : 'border-[#e8dcc8] hover:border-[#a0714a]/50'} bg-[#f5f0e6]`}>
                                {/* 날짜 헤더 */}
                                <div
                                    onClick={() => { setSelectedDate(dateStr); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task: null})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }}
                                    className={`px-2 py-2 border-b border-[#e8dcc8] flex flex-col items-center cursor-pointer hover:bg-[#e8dcc8] transition-all ${isToday ? 'bg-[#a0714a]/10' : 'bg-[#f0e9de]'}`}
                                >
                                    <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold ${isWeekend ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : isToday ? 'text-[#a0714a]' : 'text-[#a89880]'}`}>
                                        {isToday ? `${DAY_NAMES_KR[i]} ✦` : DAY_NAMES_KR[i]}
                                    </span>
                                    <span className={`text-lg font-black leading-tight ${isToday ? 'text-[#a0714a]' : (isWeekend ? 'text-[#9b4d4d]' : 'text-[#42392e]')}`}>
                                        {day.getDate()}
                                    </span>
                                    {holidayName && <span className="text-[8px] text-[#9b4d4d] truncate w-full text-center">{holidayName}</span>}
                                </div>

                                {/* 태스크 목록 */}
                                <div className="flex-1 p-1.5 flex flex-col gap-1 min-h-[80px]">
                                    {dayTasks.slice(0, 3).map(task => {
                                        const style = getBarStyle(task);
                                        const isDone = task.status === 'done';
                                        return (
                                            <div
                                                key={task.id}
                                                onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }}
                                                className={`px-1.5 py-1 rounded text-[10px] font-bold border truncate flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer hover:brightness-90 transition-all ${style.bg} ${style.text} ${isDone ? 'opacity-50 line-through decoration-current' : ''}`}
                                                title={task.details}
                                            >
                                                <span>{style.emoji}</span>
                                                <span className="truncate">{task.details || task.category?.[0] || '업무'}</span>
                                            </div>
                                        );
                                    })}
                                    {dayTasks.length > 3 && (
                                        <div className="text-[9px] text-[#a89880] text-center font-bold">+{dayTasks.length - 3}개 더</div>
                                    )}
                                    {/* 빈 칸 추가 버튼 */}
                                    <div
                                        onClick={() => { setSelectedDate(dateStr); setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task: null})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }}
                                        className="mt-auto px-1.5 py-1 rounded text-[10px] text-[#c4b49a] border border-dashed border-[#d4c4ac] text-center cursor-pointer hover:border-[#a0714a] hover:text-[#a0714a] hover:bg-[#faf6ef] transition-all"
                                    >
                                        ＋
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        );
                    })}
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* 요약 카드 */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                {statusCards.map(card => {
                    const isActive = selectedStatus === card.key;
                    return (
                        <button key={card.key} onClick={() => setSelectedStatus(isActive ? null : card.key)}
                            className={`vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl p-5 border text-left transition-all hover:shadow-md hover:-translate-y-0.5 ${isActive ? card.activeColor : 'border-[#d4c4ac]'}`}>
                            <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                                <div className={`text-xs font-bold ${isActive ? card.countColor : 'text-[#857460]'}`}>{card.label}</div>
                                {isActive && <span className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold ${card.badgeColor}`}>선택됨</span>}
                            </div>
                            <div className={`text-3xl font-black ${card.countColor}`}>{card.count}</div>
                            <div className="text-xs text-[#a89880] mt-1">{card.unit}</div>
                            <div className={`text-[10px] mt-3 font-bold transition-all ${isActive ? card.countColor : 'text-[#d4c4ac]'}`}>
                                {isActive ? '▲ 목록 닫기' : '▼ 목록 보기'}
                            </div>
                        </button>
                    );
                })}
            </div>

            {/* 펼침 목록 */}
            {selectedStatus && (
                <div className="vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl border border-[#a0714a] overflow-hidden animate-in slide-in-from-top-2 duration-200">
                    <div className="px-5 py-3 bg-[#f0e9de] border-b border-[#d4c4ac] flex items-center justify-between">
                        <h3 className="font-bold text-[#42392e] flex items-center gap-2">
                            <ClipboardList size={16} className="text-[#a0714a]"/>
                            {statusLabel[selectedStatus]} 업무 목록
                            <span className="text-xs bg-[#a0714a]/20 text-[#a0714a] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">{selectedTasks.length}건</span>
                        </h3>
                        <button onClick={() => setSelectedStatus(null)} className="p-1 rounded-full hover:bg-[#e8dcc8]"><X size={16} className="text-[#857460]"/></button>
                    </div>
                    {selectedTasks.length === 0 ? (
                        <div className="py-12 text-center">
                            <CheckCircle size={36} className="text-[#d4c4ac] mx-auto mb-3"/>
                            <p className="text-sm text-[#857460]">해당하는 업무가 없습니다.</p>
                        </div>
                    ) : (
                        <div className="divide-y divide-[#f0e9de] max-h-[360px] overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
                            {selectedTasks.map(task => {
                                const linkedPlan = plans.find(p => p.id === task.planId);
                                const statusBadge = { done: 'bg-[#5d7a5d]/20 text-[#5d7a5d]', in_progress: 'bg-[#a0714a]/20 text-[#a0714a]', todo: 'bg-[#857460]/20 text-[#857460]' };
                                const statusIcon = task.status === 'done'
                                    ? <CheckCircle size={16} className="text-[#5d7a5d] flex-shrink-0"/>
                                    : task.status === 'in_progress'
                                    ? <Activity size={16} className="text-[#a0714a] flex-shrink-0"/>
                                    : <div className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-[#d4c4ac] flex-shrink-0"/>;
                                const style = getBarStyle(task);
                                return (
                                    <div key={task.id} onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} className="flex items-center gap-4 px-5 py-3 hover:bg-[#f5f0e6] cursor-pointer transition-all group">
                                        {statusIcon}
                                        <span className="text-base flex-shrink-0">{style.emoji}</span>
                                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                                            <div className={`text-sm font-bold truncate ${task.status === 'done' ? 'line-through text-[#a89880]' : 'text-[#42392e]'}`}>{task.details || '내용 없음'}</div>
                                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-0.5">
                                                {linkedPlan && <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#f0e9de] border border-[#d4c4ac] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[#6a5d50] truncate max-w-[150px]">{linkedPlan.topic}</span>}
                                                {task.category?.map(c => <span key={c} className="text-[10px] text-[#857460]">#{c}</span>)}
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <span className="text-xs text-[#857460] flex items-center gap-1 flex-shrink-0"><User size={12}/> {task.author}</span>
                                        <span className="text-[10px] text-[#a89880] font-mono flex-shrink-0 hidden md:block">{task.workStartDate} ~ {task.workEndDate}</span>
                                        <span className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-1 rounded-full font-bold flex-shrink-0 ${statusBadge[task.status]}`}>
                                            {task.status === 'done' ? '완료' : task.status === 'in_progress' ? '진행중' : '대기'}
                                        </span>
                                        <Edit size={14} className="text-[#d4c4ac] group-hover:text-[#a0714a] transition-colors flex-shrink-0"/>
                                    </div>
                                );
                            })}
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>
            )}

            {/* 중간: 오늘 할 일 + 팀원 현황 */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-6">
                <div className="vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-[#d4c4ac]">
                    <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-[#42392e] flex items-center gap-2 mb-4"><CalendarIcon size={20} className="text-[#a0714a]"/> 오늘 할 일</h3>
                    {todayTasks.length === 0 ? (
                        <div className="text-center py-8 text-[#857460]"><CheckCircle size={32} className="mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50"/><p className="text-sm">오늘 예정된 업무가 없습니다</p></div>
                    ) : (
                        <div className="space-y-2">
                            {todayTasks.map(task => {
                                const style = getBarStyle(task);
                                return (
                                    <div key={task.id} onClick={() => { setSelectedItems(prev => ({...prev, task})); toggleModal('schedule', true); }} className="p-3 bg-[#f0e9de] rounded-xl cursor-pointer hover:bg-[#e8dcc8] transition-all border border-[#d4c4ac]">
                                        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                                            <span className="text-sm font-bold text-[#42392e] truncate flex items-center gap-1.5">
                                                <span>{style.emoji}</span>{task.details || '내용 없음'}
                                            </span>
                                            <span className="text-xs text-[#857460]">{task.author}</span>
                                        </div>
                                        {task.category && task.category.length > 0 && (
                                            <div className="flex gap-1 mt-1">{task.category.map(c => <span key={c} className="text-[10px] bg-[#a0714a]/20 text-[#a0714a] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">{c}</span>)}</div>
                                        )}
                                    </div>
                                );
                            })}
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>
                <div className="vj-card bg-[#faf6ef] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-[#d4c4ac]">
                    <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-[#42392e] flex items-center gap-2 mb-4"><User size={20} className="text-[#a0714a]"/> 팀원별 현황</h3>
